 com / 5bocqiijha— ANI (@ani_news)may 22, 2015the misuse of investigative agencies, is now an event of the past: I&B Minister Arun Jaitley— ANI (@ani_news)may 22, 2015 The government on Saturday clarified that it will be mandatory to add Aadhaar and PAN from July 1 to file income tax returns and obtain Permanent Account Number (PAN)
 sarkaar kii taraf se yah spashtikaran supreme court ke is sambandh main die faisle ke ek din baad aayaa he
 The apex court has validated the provision made in the Income Tax Act which makes Aadhaar mandatory for allotment of PAN card and filing of income tax returns, but until its constitutional bench decides on the matter of right to privacy, its implementation is partial Postponement iskar vibhaag kii niti nirmaataa sanstha kendriya pratyaksh kar board (sibiditi) ne shanivaar ko ek vaktavy jari kar spasht kiya ki supreme court ne shuukravaar ko apane faisle main keval un logon ko aanshik raahat di he, jinke paas aadhaar number nahin he athwa jinhone aadhaar main panjikaran nahin karaayaa he, aise main kar adhikari un logon ke pan ko nirast nahin karenge
 The CBDT has issued a three-point clarification regarding the Supreme Court's decision
 karadaataaon main supreme court ke faisle se kisi tarah kii ashanka ko dur karne ke liye yah spashtikaran diya gaya
 From July 1, 2017, every person who is eligible to get Aadhaar will be required to mention their Aadhaar number or mention their Aadhaar registration ID number in filing income tax return or applying for PAN
 sibiditi ne kaha he, '1 july, 2017 ko jis bhi vyakti ko pan number aavantit kiya gaya he or jis bhi vyakti ke paas aadhaar number he yaa phir vah aadhaar number lene kaa paatr he use pan ke saath aadhaar number jodne ke liye apana aadhaar number iskar prashasan ko bataanaa hoga
 ' vibhaag ne is bare main bhi spashtikaran diya he ki yadi kisi vyakti ke paas aadhaar number nahin he athwa aadhaar number kaa ullekh nahin kiya jaataa he, to uskaa kya hoga
 The department has said, 'the apex court has given only partial relief in this case
 yah raahat un logon ko di gai he, jinke paas aadhaar nahin he yaa jo philhal aadhaar nahin lenaa chaah rahe hai
 In the case of such people, the PAN number will not be canceled, so that they do not have to bear the brunt of other rules not mentioning the PAN number under the Income Tax Act
 ' a senior income tax official told that if the PAN is canceled, the person concerned will not be able to carry out his normal banking and financial operations, hence this relief has been granted
 lekin yah spasht kiya gaya he ki 1 july se iskar ritern daakhil karne or nayaa pan yadi bananaa he to aadhaar kaa ullekh karnaa anivaary hoga
 The senior official said that Friday's decision of the apex court has been studied by the officials of Law Ministry, Ministry of Finance, CBDT and Income Tax Department and only after that the clarification has been issued
 tippaniyan Under the Finance Act 2017, the government made it mandatory for taxpayers to mention Aadhaar number or Aadhaar registration application number while filing income tax returns
 iske saath hi ek july 2017 se pan ke liye aavedan karne main bhi aadhaar kaa ullekh anivaary kar diya gaya
 Income Tax Department 1 so far
 16 karod aadhaar number ko pan ke saath jod chukaa he
 (apart from the headline, this news has not been edited by the NDTV team, it has been published directly from the Syndicate feed
 ) The Central Board of Direct Taxes (CBDT), the policy making body of the Income Tax Department, issued a statement on Saturday clarifying that the Supreme Court in its judgment on Friday only gave partial relief to those who do not have an Aadhaar number or who have Aadhaar The tax authorities will not cancel the PAN of those people who have not registered
 sibiditi ne supreme court ke faisle ke bare main teen binduon kaa spashtikaran jari kiya he
 This explanation was given to the taxpayers to remove any apprehension from the Supreme Court's decision
 1 july, 2017 se prayek vyakti jo aadhaar paane kaa paatr he uske liye iskar ritern daakhil karne yaa phir pan ke liye aavedan karne main apane aadhaar number kaa ullekh athwa aadhaar panjikaran sambandhi idi number kaa ullekh karnaa anivaary hoga
 The CBDT has said, 'on July 1, 2017, any person who has been allotted a PAN number and whoever has an Aadhaar number or is eligible to get an Aadhaar number is required to add their Aadhaar number with PAN The number has to be reported to the Income Tax Administration
 ' The department has also given clarification about what will happen if a person does not have an Aadhaar number or if the Aadhaar number is not mentioned
 vibhaag ne kaha he, 'is maamle main sheersh adaalat ne keval aanshik raahat di he
 This relief has been given to those who do not have Aadhaar or who are not willing to take Aadhaar at present
 aise logon ke maamle main pan number nirast nahin kiya jayega, taaki iskar adhinium ke tahat pan number kaa ullekh nahin karne sambandhi duusare niyamon kaa khamiyaja unhen nahin bhugatna pade
 ' ek varisht iskar adhikari ne bataaya yadi pan ko nirast kar diya jaataa he, to sambandhit vyakti apane saamaanya banking or vittiya parichaalan nahin kar paaegaa, isliye yah raahat di gai he
 But it has been clarified that it will be mandatory to file Aadhaar return from July 1 and mention Aadhaar if a new PAN is to be created

Who is the most favorite leader of the people of India? Taking similar questions, India Today and Nielsen's team scoured the entire country and the results that came out are astonishing
 survey ke mutabik sabase zyada logon kii raay yahi he ki gujarat ke mukhyamantri narendra modi sabit honge sabase achche pradhanmantri

 gujarat ke mukhyamantri narendra modi ke nishane par dilli kaa takht he to public ke mood par bhi chal rahaa he modi kaa magic
 In the BJP, Modi is the biggest contender for the PM in waiting, so most of the people of the country want Modi to be the next Prime Minister
 ye ham nahin kehete
 These results are from the latest survey of India Today and Nielsen
 survey ke mutabik21 fisadi logon kii raay main narendra modi desh ke sabase achche pradhanmantri sabit honge
 The India Today and Nielsen survey asked the public one more question - if the BJP wins the Gujarat Assembly elections, will the BJP put forward Narendra Modi's name for the Prime Minister's candidature? In response, 55 percent people said yes, while 25 percent said no
 logon par chalaa narendra modi kaa magicanarendra modi kaa magic kis tarah logon par chalaa he, ye aap survey ke aankadon main dekh sakate hai

 is baat main bhi koi shaq nahin he ki kin raajnneetik tatwon ne hinsa ko badhaava or uksaava diya
 There was a deliberate attempt to show the strength of the majority in order to give a message to the Muslim communities living in the area that they have to live in fear, accept the cultural decrees of the majority community and consider themselves inferior to them
 khat main ye bhi likhaa gaya he ki police or naagarik prashasan vikrut raajnneetik tantra ke aage jhuk chukaa he
 They have forgotten their primary loyalty to the Constitution and the rule of law, while their constitutional status gives them unprecedented power
 agar wo hindutv brigade ke badhate dar ko rokane ke liye kadam uthaate to hinsa ko nishchit hi roka ja saktaa tha
 But he not only allowed the hooligans to rise and encouraged them to gain political power, but also helped to remove their fear of law from their mindless action
 ab bhi agar mukhya sachiv, dijipi, grih sachiv, dm or zila police adhikari ek saath khadey ho jaaen to is ghaatak raajnneetik agenda kaa pardaafaash kiya ja saktaa he, iske masterminds ko pahachaanaa ja saktaa he or hinsa karne waalon ko kathghare main khadaa kiya ja saktaa he
 These officers have the opportunity to fulfill the oath of the Constitution and fulfill the expectations that citizens have from higher civil services
 tippaniyan The letter calls for the Prime Minister to write that our Prime Minister, who does not get tired in his election campaigns saying that the Constitution of India is the only book he worships, is also silent in this matter while his elected Chief Minister Playing with the same constitution
 ye saafe he ki sangh parivaar ke liye sanvaidhanik naitikta kaa koi mulya nahin he or wo bahusnkhyakon ke dabadabe ke vichaar ko maanata he
 This is a very serious time and we cannot just leave it like that
 ham sabhi nagarikon se nafrat or bantwaare kii is raajnneeti ke kilaaf ek hone kii maang karte hai
 We demand that the Chief Minister of Uttar Pradesh resign for failing to abide by the Constitution he has sworn to implement
 ham jaanate hai ki ye tabhi ho paaegaa jab ham milakar janabhaawanaaon ko ubhaaren or unhen apane kaam ke liye zimmedaari kaa ahsaas karaate hue istife ke liye majaboor karen
 We would like to remind the Chief Secretary, DGP, Home Secretary and all members of the higher civil services that it is their constitutional obligation to establish the rule of law without fear, instead of perverse orders of their political masters
 isi ke saath elahabaad hycourt se aagrah kiya gaya he ki vah is ghatana kaa swat: sangyaan yani suo motu cognizance len or apni nigaraanee main ek nyaayik jaanch kaa aadesh den
 The Supreme Court's decision came after a long time, but we discussed it only when the Bombay High Court was ordered to bail
 faizan mustafa hamaare saath the or unhone is baat kii samiksha kii thi
 In the prime time of 17 January 2017, Faizan Mustafa gave his opinion on the order of the Bombay High Court judge
 insaaf kii bhi apni raajnneeti he
 Debaters argue on behalf of Hindus, argue on behalf of Muslims
 lekin jo peedit hota he uske kaam koi dharm nahin aata he
 Neither Islam nor Hindu
 wo akelaa ladata hua chand logon ke bharose ke sahare jeeta he
 Sob isliye insaaf ke liye jashn manaane waalon ko ek baar jagadish cor se poochna chahie ki 34 saal sangharsh unhone kiya yaa tivi main aane vaale pravaktaaon ne kiya
 Rather, if they do not meet, they should ask Mohsin's mother Shabana Sadiq Sheikh, if they cannot find it, then they should ask Rajni ji, wife of Inspector Subodh Kumar Singh, who was killed in Bulandshahr
 shabana or rajani kii ladaai bhi zakiya jaafaree or jagadish cor kii tarah akele kii ladaai he
 You must remember that picture of the crowd, the mob gathered in the name of the cow killed Inspector Subodh Kumar Singh
 16-17 din ho gaye mukhya aaropee nahin pakadaa gaya
 Meanwhile, the main accused also released a statement through whatsapp which went on TV
 is cese main police ke varisht adhikariyon kaa tabadalaa ho gaya lekin mukhya aaropee nahin pakadaa gaya
 The Chief Minister had also called a meeting after the incident about which there was no mention of Subodh Kumar Singh when the press release was issued, that strict action should be taken against those who killed cow
 baad main mukhyamantri adityanath ne peedit parivaar ko lakhanu bulaayaa, subodh kumaar singh kii patni rajani, unke bete unase milane gaye lekin abhi tak mukhya aaropee nahin pakadaa gaya he
 Today, more than 80 retired officials have written an open letter regarding the murder of Subodh Kumar Singh
 inamen iesces, iees or ipies, van seva or rajasav seva ke adhikari hai
 Some have been ambassadors in many important countries
 is suchi main purv rashtriya suraksha salaahkaar shiv shankar menon bhi hai
 The letter criticizes Chief Minister Aditya Nath, accusing him of favoring bigotry and demanding his resignation
 in afasaron ne likhaa he ki ve kisi raajnneetik dal se nahin hai
 Do not believe in any ideology other than the values of the constitution
 is patr kaa kuch hissaa aapke liye padhanaa chahta hum- 3 disambar, 2018 ko uttarapradesh ke bulandshahr main durbhaavna ke saath bheed kii hinsa ko anjaam diya gaya
 In this, a brave officer of the UP police, who was trying to calm the crowd, was brutally murdered
 ye nafrat kii raajnneeti kii disha main sabase bhayanak mode ban gaya
 It shows that Uttar Pradesh, the most populous state in the country, has kept the fundamental principles of governance, constitutional ethics and human social behavior at bay
 rajya ke mukhyamantri kattarta or bahusankhyakwaad ke varchasv ko badhaava de rahe hai
 This is an agenda that dominates everything else
 khat ke mutabik aisi ghatnaayen uttarapradesh main pehle bhi hui hai lekin abhi tak hamen vishwaas tha ki jab bhi koi raajnneetik dal sarkaar banaata he to wo pakshpaat bhare raajnneetik agenda ko alag rakhkar zimmedaari ke saath shashan karata he taaki uski raajnneetik sweekaaryata bade
 But before the Bulandshahr incident, there have been constant attempts to intimidate and isolate the Muslim community in UP
 yogi adityanath ke mukhyamantri rahete hamaara wo vishwaas galat sabit hua he or gundgardee or thagi shashan kii mukhyadhara main shaamil ho gaye hai taaki na sirf alpsankhyakon ko daraaya ja sake balki har us vyakti, police or prashasan ko sabak sikhaaya ja sake jo alpsankhyak samudaay ke saath barabari kaa vyavhaar karne kii himmat kare

 Justice also has its own politics
 bahes karne vaale hindu kii taraf se bahes karte hai, muslim kii taraf se bahes karte hai
 But whoever suffers, no religion is used
 na islam na hindu
 He lives by fighting the trust of a few while fighting alone
 sisakata he
 So those celebrating for justice should once ask Jagdish Kaur whether she struggled for 34 years or the spokespersons appearing in TV
 balki wo na milen to unhen mohsin kii maa shabana sadiq sheikh se poochna chahie, wo bhi na mil paaen to bulandshahr main maar die gaye inspector subodh kumaar singh kii patni rajani ji se poochna chahie
 The battle of Shabana and Rajni is also a lonely battle like Zakia Jaffrey and Jagdish Kaur
 aapako bheed kii vah tasviir to yaad hi hogi, gaay ke naam par jamaa bheed ne inspector subodh kumaar singh kii hatya kar di
 It has been 16–17 days since the main accused has not been arrested
 is bich mukhya aaropee ne whatsap ke zarie ek bayaan bhi jari kiya jo tivi par chalaa
 In this case, senior police officers were transferred but the main accused was not arrested
 mukhyamantri ne ghatana ke baad ek baithak bhi bulaai thi jiske bare main press release jari hui to subodh kumaar singh ke bare main koi zikr nahin tha, is baat kaa tha ki gau hatya karne waalon par sakht karrwai kii jaae
 Later Chief Minister Adityanath called the victim's family to Lucknow, Subodh Kumar Singh's wife Rajni, his sons went to meet him but the main accused has not yet been caught
 aaj hi subodh kumaar singh kii hatya ko lekar 80 se adhik sevanivrutt adhikariyon ne khulaa patr likhaa he
 These include officers of IFS, IAS and IPS, Forest Service and Revenue Service
 kuch kai mahatvapurn mulkon main rajdoot rah chuke hai
 Former National Security Advisor Shiv Shankar Menon is also on this list
 is patr main mukhyamantri aditya nath kii aalochana kii gai he, un par dharmandhta kaa paksh lene kaa aarope lagaaya gaya he or istife kii maang kii gai he
 These officers have written that they are not from any political party
 samvidhan ke mulyon ke alaava kisi or vichaardhaara main yakeen nahin rakhte
 i want to read some part of this letter for you - On December 3, 2018, mob violence was carried out in Bulandshahr, Uttar Pradesh with malice
 isamen bheed ko shant karne kii koshish kar rahe upi police ke ek bahadur afasar kii nrushans hatya kar di gai
 This became the most terrible turn in the direction of hate politics
 ye dikhaata he ki desh ke sabase aabaadi vaale rajya uttarapradesh main shashan ke moulik siddhanton, sanvaidhanik naitikta or maanviya saamaajik vyavhaar ko taak par rakh diya gaya he
 The chief minister of the state is promoting the domination of fundamentalism and majoritarianism
 ye ek aisa agenda he jo duusari har chiz par haaavee he
 According to the letter such incidents have happened in Uttar Pradesh before but till now we believed that whenever a political party forms a government, it rules with responsibility keeping aside the partisan political agenda to increase its political acceptability
 lekin bulandshahr kii ghatana se pehle upi main muslim samudaay ko daraane or alag-thalag karne kii lagaataar koshishen hoti rahi hai
 With Yogi Adityanath as the Chief Minister, our faith has been proved wrong and hooliganism and cheating have joined the mainstream of governance to not only intimidate the minorities but to teach a lesson to every person, police and administration who along with the minority community Dare to behave equally
 jab tak inspector subodh kumaar singh kii hatya ke maamle main jaanch puri nahin ho jaati tab tak kisi nattejey par pahunchnaa jaldbaazi hogi lekin isamen koi shaq nahin he ki jis tarah unki hatya hui usamen kuch bhi swaabhaavik yaa swat: sfoort nahin tha
 There is also no doubt about which political elements encouraged and instigated the violence
 jaanboojhkar bahusnkhyakon kii taaqat ko dikhaane kii koshish hui taaki ilaake main rahane vaale muslim samudaayon ko sandesh diya ja sake ki unhen dar main rahanaa hoga, wo bahusankhyak samudaay ke saanskrithik farmaanon ko maane or khud ko unase kamatar maane
 It is also written in the letter that the police and civil administration have succumbed to the distorted political system
 wo samvidhan ke prati apni praathmik vafadaari or kaanoon ke raaj ko bhul chuke hai jabaki unka sanvaidhanik darja unhen abhootpurv taaqat detaa he
 If they had taken steps to curb the growing fear of the Hindutva brigade, the violence could have been definitely prevented
 lekin unhone naa sirf gundgardee karne waalon ke hausale ko badhane diya or unhen raajnneetik taaqat hasil karne diya balki apni lachar karrwai se unke man se kaanoon ke dar ko hataane main bhi madad kii
 Even now, if the Chief Secretary, DGP, Home Secretary, DM and district police officers stand together, this deadly political agenda can be exposed, its masterminds can be identified and the perpetrators of violence should be put in the dock Can
 in adhikariyon ke saamne samvidhan kii shapath ko puraa karne kaa mauka he or ucch naagarik sevaaon se nagarikon ko jo ummiden hai unhen puraa karne kaa avasar he
 The comments khat main pradhanmantri kaa aahvaan karte hue likhaa gaya he ki hamaare pradhanmantri jo apane chunavi abhiyaanon main ye kehete nahin thakte ki bharat kaa samvidhan hi ekmaatr kitaab he jisaki wo puja karte hai, wo bhi is maamle main chuppi saadhe hue hai jabaki unke chune hue mukhyamantri usee samvidhan ke saath khilwaad kar rahe hai
 It is clear that constitutional morality has no value for the Sangh Parivar and it considers the idea of majority domination
 ye ek bahut hi gambhir samay he or ham ise yon hi nahin chhod sakate
 We demand all citizens to unite against this politics of hate and division
 ham maang karte hai ki uttarapradesh ke mukhyamantri samvidhan ke paalan main naakaam rahane ke liye istifa den jis samvidhan ko lagu karne kii unhone shapath khai he
 We know that this will happen only when we together raise public sentiments and force them to resign, making them feel responsible for their work
 ham mukhya sachiv, dijipi, grih sachiv or ucch naagarik sevaaon ke sabhi sadasyon ko yaad dilaanaa chaahate hai ki ye unka sanvaidhanik daayitv he ki wo apane raajnneetik aakaaon ke vikrut adeshon ke bajaay bina dare kaanoon kaa raaj sthapit karen
 Simultaneously, the Allahabad High Court has been requested to take suo motu cognizance of this incident and order a judicial inquiry under its supervision

aaj saunpega states report12:00 AM gujarat: vadodara main baari barish ke kaaran aaj skulon kii chuttee12:00 AM 4 agast tak ke liye amarnath yatra sthagit Despite the excellent bowling of Ashwin and Harbhajan, the only Test draw between India and Bangladesh was done
 aswin ke paanch or bhajji ke teen wicket ke dam par bharat ne bangladesh ko foloon ke liye majaboor to kar diya, lekin match ke paanchon din barish ke damdaar pradarshan ke kaaran test jeet nahin paaya
 During the match, more than 250 overs fell due to rain, if the game could have been played for the entire three days, then probably the Indian team would have won the match
 viraat kohli kii aguai vaali bhartiya team ne is match main khel ke sabhi vibhaagon main dabadabaa banaae rakhaa, or iskaa phayda use ekadivasiy siries main milegaa jahaan team india bade hue manobal ke saath utregi
 India declared their first innings by scoring 462 runs for six wickets, in response to which Bangladesh started the fifth and final day by 111 runs for three wickets
 pehle satr kaa khel barish kii bhent chadhane ke baavjood bhartiya spinneron nen bangladesh kii team ko 256 ranon par dher kar unhen foloon ke liye majaboor kar diya
 Imranul KS scored the highest score of 72 runs in the first innings for Bangladesh but it was Litan Das who won the hearts of all, playing his first Test match, wicketkeeper batsman Litton Dasne scored a quick 45 in 45 balls
 unhone apni pari main aath chauke or ek chakka jamaaya
 For India, Ashwin took five wickets for 87 runs in 25 overs while Harbhajan 17
 5 over main 64 ran dekar teen wicket hasil kiye
 Harbhajan became the ninth most successful bowler in the history of Test as soon as he took the second wicket in this Test, beating Pakistan's Wasim Akram
 din ke 30 over baaki rahete foloon ke baad khilne utari bangladesh ne jab duusari pari main 15 over main bina wicket khoe 23 ran bana liye the tabhi donon captain match drow khatm karne par raji ho gaye
 Bangladesh's Setemim Iqbal was unbeaten on 16 while Imranul KS scored seven runs
 bharat ke shikhar dhawan ko unki 173 ranon kii pari ke liye main of da match kaa aword diya gaya
 From input language shina bora hatyakand jitna rishton ke pench main ulajhaa he, uski jaanch main mumbai police ayukta rakesh maaria kii dilchaspee bhi utana hi hairaan karne vaali he
 The discussion even goes so far that Rakesh Maria waited for the right time for months to get the dead corpses of the Sheena massacre and then one by one got his favorite police officers posted at Bandra Division and Khar Police Station
 khaar police kii kahani main haalanki jaanch kii shuruyaat 21 agast 2015 bataai gai he, jab carter road par police gast ke dauraan dryver shamvar pinturam raay avaidh pistaul ke saath giraftaar hua
 In questioning, he revealed the murder of Sheena Bora
 yani teen saal puraani hatya kii aisi gutthi jo police fil main bhi darj nahin thi, jiske taar mumbai se kolkata or guwahati tak se jude hai
 In which there is such a screw of relationships, which is difficult to understand
 mumbai main ab tak kii sabase sansanikhej murder mistry achaanak se police ke haath lag gai, lekin police mahakme se lekar media tak main charchaa kuch or he
 Because on 26 August 2012, in his cabin, talking to journalists, Police Commissioner Rakesh Maria himself has said that we were working on this for two months
 matlab saaf he ki shina kii hatya kii tip mumbai police ko bahut pehle hi lag gai thi
 The discussion even goes so far that no one else got the tip of Mumbai Police Commissioner Rakesh Maria himself
 or vah itani satik thi ki aparaadh kii shuruyaat koun se thane main hui he yah bhi pataa tha
 If this is true, then the question is, who is that person? And why did he hide Raj for three years? maamla media se jude ek bade shaks ke parivaar se judaa tha or jisaki hatya kii tip thi uske laapata hone kii shikaayat tak kahin darj nahin karai gai thi
 Therefore it was necessary to keep every step blazing
 to kya isiilie mumbai police ayukta rakesh maaria ne is maamle kii jaanch ke liye hi ek-ek kar apane chahete or bharosemand afasaron ko pehle bandra divijan main tainaat karavaaya? ACP Sanjay Kadam, close to Maria, who was in the Economic Offenses Wing, came into the Bandra Division a few months ago as ACP
 or sabase badi baat police nireekshak dinesh kadam kii, jo 1993 bam dhamaakon kii jaanch ke samay se hi rakesh maaria ke khaas maane jate hai
 When Rakesh Maria was the ATS Chief, Dinesh Kadam was also in the ATS
 us samay unka tabadalaa nagpur kar diya gaya tha, lekin maaria ne ye kahkar tabadalaa rukvaa diya ki dinesh kadam jaise afasaron kii aties main jarurat he
 Now he is also posted in the same Khar police station, where the Sheena murder case is being investigated
 bataaya ja rahaa he ki jaanch team ke sarvesarva dinesh kadam hi hai
 The news even goes so far that the core team led by Dinesh Kadam is reporting directly to Police Commissioner Rakesh Maria
 vaise khaar police thane ke incharge dattatraya bargude bhi 26 / 11 aatanki hamale kii jaanch main rakesh maaria ke adheen krim branch main kaam kar chuke hai
 Although Maria herself would call it coincidental, it is rare
 tippaniyan The biggest thing is that usually the investigation of such high profile and complicated murder mystery is often given to the Mumbai Crime Branch, but the crime branch has been kept away from this case so far
 khud police ayukta rakesh maaria or kanoon vyavastha ke sanyukt ayukta deven bharti kai baar khaar police stesan main deraa daale rahe hai
 Rakesh Maria himself has made several rounds of questioning of the accused
 haalanki yah bhi sahi he ki rakesh maaria duusare maamalon main bhi aropiyon se poochtacha karte rahe hai
 The entire investigation is being kept secret so that small police officers are far away, even top officers are avoiding talking to the media
 or to or maamle se judi khabaron kii pushti yaa khandan karne vaala bha koi nahin he, jabaki kolkata or guwahati se khabaron kii bauchhaar ho rahi he
 The story of the Khar police, however, begins the investigation on 21 August 2015, when driver Shamwar Pinturam Rai was arrested with an illegal pistol during a police patrol on Carter Road
 poochtacha main usne shina bora kii hatya kaa khulaasa kiya
 That is, such a three-year old murder case which was not even recorded in the police file, whose wires are connected from Mumbai to Kolkata and Guwahati
 jisamen rishton kaa aisa pench he, jise samaj paanaa mushkil ho rahaa he
 The most sensational murder mystery of all time in Mumbai was suddenly caught by the police, but the discussion from the police department to the media is something else
 kyonki 26 agast 2012 ko apane cabin main patrakaron se baatcheet main khud police ayukta rakesh maaria kah chuke hai ki ham do maheene se is par kaam kar rahe the
 It is clear that the tip of Sheena's murder was found by the Mumbai Police long back
 charchaa to yahaan tak he ki tip kisi or ne nahin khud mumbai police ayukta rakesh maaria ko mili thi
 And she was so precise that the crime started in which police station was also aware
 agar ye baat sahi he to sawaal he ki vah shaks koun he? or teen saal tak usne raaj ko kyon chipa kar rakhaa? The case was related to the family of a prominent media person and the complaint regarding the disappearance of the one who had the tip of the murder was not lodged anywhere
 isliye har kadam phoonk-phoonk kar rakhana jaruri tha
 So is this why Mumbai Police Commissioner Rakesh Maria got his favorite and trusted officers posted in Bandra Division one by one to investigate the matter? maaria ke kareebi asipi sanjay kadam jo aarthik aparaadh shakha main the, vah kuch maheene pehle bandra divijan main asipi banakar aae hai
 And the biggest thing was that of Police Inspector Dinesh Kadam, who is considered to be special of Rakesh Maria since the time of investigation of 1993 bomb blasts
 jab rakesh maaria aties chif the, tab dinesh kadam bhi aties main the
 At that time, he was transferred to Nagpur, but Maria stopped transfer saying that officers like Dinesh Kadam were needed in the ATS
 ab wo bhi usee khaar police stesan main tainaat hai, jahaan shina murder cese kii jaanch ho rahi he
 It is being told that the survey team's survey is Dinesh Kadam
 khabar to yahaan tak he ki dinesh kadam ke netritv main bani kor team sidhe police ayukta rakesh maaria ko report kar rahi he
 However, in charge of Khar police station, Dattatraya Bargude has also worked in the Crime Branch under Rakesh Maria in the investigation of 26 / 11 terror attack
 haalanki khud maaria bhi ise ittefaq hi kahenge, lekin aisa ittefaq virale hi hota he
 The comments sabase badi baat ki amuman is tarah kii hai profile or pechida murder mistry kii jaanch aksar mumbai krim branch ko de di jaati he, lekin is cese se krime branch ko abhi tak dur hi rakhaa gaya he
 Commissioner of Police Rakesh Maria himself and Deven Bharti, Joint Commissioner of Law and Order, are camping at Khar Police Station several times
 rakesh maaria ne khud bhi aropiyon se kai daur kii poochtacha kii he
 However, it is also true that Rakesh Maria has been questioning the accused in other cases as well
 puri jaanch ko is kadar gupt rakhaa ja rahaa he ki chote police afasar to dur kii baat he, aalaa afasar bhi media se baat karne se batch rahe hai
 Moreover, there is no one to confirm or refute the news related to the case, while the news is being bombarded from Kolkata and Guwahati
